 isiilie yah hindi sahitya kii sabase kathin vidhaon main se ek he
 Eminent critic Chittaranjan Mishra said that the fine essay is an expression of the soul
 ise yon bhi kah sakate hai ki apni aatma kii awaz ko duusare tak pahunchaane kii koshish hi lalit niabandh he
 Fine essays are news of the soul
 atah ise aatmavyanjak niabandh bhi kaha jaataa he
 The excellence of the fine essay depends on the harmony of knowledge and experience
 mishra ne kaha ki lok tatva main sabhi baaten samahit hoti hai, vaise hi lalit niabandh main sahitya ke sabhi tatva shaamil hote hai
 That is, the Fine Essay is the largest refuge of folk elements in literature
 prakhyat hindi lekhak shyamsundar dube ne udghaatan vaktavy main lalit niabandh ke saamne khadi chunautiyon kii charchaa karte hue kaha ki hindi sahitya kii kisi bhi vidha ne itani baadhaon kaa saamana nahin kiya hoga
 He spoke of the powerful readers with reference to the popularity of fine essays
 aage unhone kaha ki itane prashnon, sandehon ke baavjood bhi agar lalit niabandh kaa vikaas ho rahaa he to yah uski jeevatata or samarthyavan hone kaa hi saboot he
 Jugalbandi of folk and scripture is the background of a good fine essay and a fine essay is the process of enriching the readers from the linguistic point of view
 unhone yah bhi spasht kiya ki sanathan smritiyon se jodne kii samarthy keval lalit niabandh main he
 Eminent Hindi writer Shriram Parihar gave a detailed definition of the Fine Essay in his seed statement, and said that the mode developed between scripture and creation is the Fine Essay
 lalit niabandh kaal kii chakree sthiti kaa anusaran karata he or unamem jivan kii vyapaktaa hoti he
 That is, the mode of revealing the expression of emotion and thought in the Ramayana language is the Fine Essay

 Krishna Kumar Singh said in his article that harmony between folk and erudition is necessary only then fine essays will be eligible

 Investigation revealed that the auxiliary power unit (APU) of the aircraft was not functioning
 jisaki vajah se ingine saamaanya rup se start nahin ho rahaa tha
 The pilot started an engine aircraft's APU was not working
 isi dauraanpayalat ne ek ingine start kar diya
 In fact, when one of the aircraft's engines starts, its external power source is disconnected
 jisase vimaan ko peeche taraf dhakka lagata he
 The process of starting another engine is then followed by the running engine
 mana ja rahaa he ki isi prakriya ke dauraan yah haadasa hua
 Another reason for the accident was in Air India aircraft AI 619 in the parking bow, but it did not have parking brakes

The questions are very serious, whose answers are yet to come
 australia ne uttarakhand main kharaab mausam ke maddenzar bharat ke liye yatra paraamarsh ko apadet karte hue apane nagarikon se soochna ke liye media par najar rakhane or sthaneey adhikariyon kii salaah kaa anusaran karne ko kaha he
 The Department of Foreign Affairs and Trade (DFAT) amended the consultation on Tuesday, saying, there have been reports of landslides in Uttarkashi and Gangotri
 yadi aap prabhavit ilaake main hai, to apane bachaav ke liye media kii soochna par najar rakhen or sthaneey adhikariyon kii salaah maane
 It said that the annual monsoon rains from June to October could cause terrible floods or landslides, especially in Uttar Pradesh, Bihar, Andhra Pradesh and Karnataka
 tippaniyan The advisory states that even before this, floods have affected millions of people, killing many people
 is samay taaje pani or bhojan kii aapurti main kami aa sakati he
 Even after the flood waters recede, there is a risk of disease arising from water contamination
 parivahan or sanchaar dhaancha bhi prabhavit ho saktaa he
 Australia said in the ongoing consultation, if you are traveling in monsoon, contact your tour operator to find out if the tourism services have not been interrupted where you need to go
 smart traveler website par jari paraamarsh main kaha gaya he, ham aatankwaad , nagarikon ke bich ashaanti, aparaadh or sadak durghatnaon ke khatre ke maddenzar australia ke logon ko bharat main behad saavdhaanee baratane kii salaah dete hai
 In the consultation, as before, tourists have been asked to exercise caution in Ladakh in Jammu and Kashmir and to reconsider their plans to travel to Jammu and Srinagar in view of the continuous armed conflict, terrorist activities and violent demonstrations

 If you are in the affected area, keep an eye on the media information and follow the advice of the local authorities for your protection
 isamen kaha gaya he ki june se oktober tak vaarshik monsoon ke kaaran varsha se khaastaur se uttar pradesh, bihar, andhra pradesh or karnataka main bhayanak baadh aa sakati he yaa bhuskhalan ho saktaa he
 The comments paraamarsh main kaha gaya he, isse purv bhi baadh ne lakhon logon ko prabhavit kiya he, jisase kai log maare gaye hai
 Freshwater and food supplies may decline at this time
 baadh ke pani ke kam ho jane ke baad bhi jal ke sankraman se paidaa hone vaali beemaari kaa khatra bana rahata he
 Transport and communication infrastructure may also be affected
 australia ne jari paraamarsh main kaha, yadi aap monsoon main yatra kar rahe hai to apane tour oparator se yah pataa lagane ke liye sampark karen ki jahaan aapako janaa he, vahaan paryaton sevaayen to baadhit nahin hui hai

 ) narendra modi jab 26 may, 2014 ko pradhanmantri pad kii shapath lene vaale the
 Hours before that, 40 people lost their lives and more than a hundred were injured in the Gorakhdham Express accident in Sant Kabirnagar, Uttar Pradesh
 modi ko shapath lene ke pehle us par samvednaa jaahir kerani padi
 So, he immediately realized the plight of the railway
 shaayad yahi vajah rahi hogi ki modi sarkaar ke pehle railway mantri sadanand gauda ne shapath lene ke baad hi kaha, ''railway kii sangraksha sarvopari he or puraani patariyon or pulon kii marammat praathamikta he
 "but in almost six months before Gowda could still do something, on November 10, 2014, the responsibility of rejuvenation of the railway was handed over to Suresh Prabhu
 suresh prabhu ne bhi pulon or patariyon kii marammat or railway ke aadhunikeekaran kii baat kii
 For this, the journey was made expensive by stating the need of money
 lekin ek ke baad ek durghatana ne railway sangraksha kii kalai khol di to suresh prabhu ko istipha dekar vidaa hona padaa
 Then, on 3 September 2017, Piyush Goyal was given the responsibility of the railway department
 na haadase ruke, na suraksha durust karne kii khaas pahal dikhi
 So, during the nearly 44-month tenure of the Modi government, a total of 27 train accidents killed 259 people and injured 899
 yani har do maheene main 1 rail durghatana hui
 So, 1 for Railways in this time budget
 48 lakh karod ru
 About 50 per cent in the provision of Rs 73,065 crore
 sirf sangraksha ke liye he (jisamen rail sangraksha kosh bhi shaamil he)

 durghatnaayen rokna praathamikta he jo trek rinyawl ke bina sambhav nahin he

 "railway board ke ek maujuuda sadsy sangraksha mad main adhik fund kii vyavastha ko acha to bataa rahe hai lekin ise naakaafi maanate hai

 " aise main sangraksha main hui chook ke liye jimmedaari tay karnaa kathin hota he
 The safety fund is spent in different departments
 masalan, patariyon kii marammat, pulon kii marammat, signling vyavastha, raling stock kaa rakrakhaav, stoff kii training vagairah
 But in the leprosy, there is no coordination between the guardians of these departments
 haalanki inke bich majboot talmail kis kadar jaruri he, yah isi se samajha ja saktaa he ki agar roling stock kaa rakrakhaav thik he magar patariyon kaa rakrakhaav thik nahin he to rail yatayaat surakshit nahin he
 Therefore uniformity in safety is necessary
 matlab yah ki phulpruf sangraksha ke liye iske liye alag se vibhaag jaruri he
 The second hole in safety is the acute shortage of staff in this item
 railway sangraksha ke kaam main 7,46,676 karmchaaree lage hai
 These include gangmen, gatemen, etc
 abhi 1,24,201 karmchaariyon kii or jarurat he
 These staff are needed to overcome problems such as cracks in tracks, fish plate imperfections and sabotage
 rail rajyamantri manoj sinha kehete hai, ''sangraksha ko lekar railway main lagaataar kaam ho rahaa he
 The work to fill the vacant posts is going on
 patariyon kii mashiinon se monitering ho rahi he, adhikariyon or karmchaariyon kii jimmedaari tay kii ja rahi he
 In this budget, Railways have got 3 times more funds than before which will be spent on safety and modernization
 "lekin pech kai hai
 Even if the budget provision for modernization and safety of railways is properly accepted, then the question arises why no time frame has been fixed? On this, officials of the Railway Board say that the time frame for these works cannot be fixed
 haa, itnaa jarur he ki jaise-jaise kaam hota jayega, trainon ke parichaalan par iskaa asar padegaa
 Officials say the 63,000-km railway line passes through 1,219 sections
 inamen 492 section aise hai jis par trephic lod 100 fisadi se adhik he
 That is, the traffic load is at its peak at about 42,000 km of track
 ek hi trek par malgadee bhi chalati he, rajdhani-shatabdi jaisi superfast or local train bhi chalati hai
 In such a situation, it is very difficult to operate the trains with time and safety
 train durghatnaon kii ek badi vajah maanviya bhul bhi he
 That is, in every case, we cannot say that accidents happen due to the fault of the tracks or due to the shortfalls in the rolling stock
 adhikariyon kaa daawa he ki malgadipoon ke avaagaman ke liye dedicated fret coridor kaa nirmaan teji se chal rahaa he
 The completion of this work will reduce the traffic pressure on the rail tracks
 aise main hyspid train chalaanaa bhi aasaan hoga or rail yatra adhik surakshit bhi hogi
